         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="db">
           db
          </span>
         </h2>
         <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r23889" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
         <div class="movedata hover-bg-grey-03">
          <div class="movedata-labels">
           <div class="movedata-name has-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Name
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The name of the move in the English localization.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Most often directly from the in-game movelist, but can also be a community name.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Alt
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             Other inputs that also perform this move, written in
             <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
              notation
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-input-ctn">
            <p>
             <span class="movedata-inputLead">
             </span>
             <span class="movedata-input">
              <span class="tooltip-label">
               <b>
                Input
               </b>
              </span>
              <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
               The input to perform the move, written in
               <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
                notation
               </a>
               . This is often used as the move's name.
               <span class="tooltip-hr">
               </span>
               For strings, the input of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
              </span>
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-threat">
           <div class="movedata-target-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-targetLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-target">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Hit level
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a href="/t/Hit_level" title="Hit level">
               hit level
              </a>
              of the move.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Capital letters mean it hits
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Grounded" title="Grounded">
               grounded
              </a>
              .
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the hit level of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-damage-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-damageLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-damage">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Damage
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              How much
              <a href="/t/Damage" title="Damage">
               damage
              </a>
              the move does without any modifiers.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the damage of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-range">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Range
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The maximum
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Range" title="Range">
              range
             </a>
             recorded of the move hitting Lars on-axis. (For
             <i>
              Tekken 7
             </i>
             , it's vs Heihachi.) Assume an error of about Â±0.03.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , this is the range of the whole string.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             This measurement shouldn't on its own be used to compare characters: larger characters get more "range" by this measure, but their
             <i>
              opponents
             </i>
             do too.
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-frames">
           <div class="movedata-tracks left">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Left Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's left.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              right for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-tracks right">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Right Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's right.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              left for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-block">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Block
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on block.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move can't be blocked (e.g., an unblockable or an aerial attack).
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For breakable
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage when the throw is broken.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-hit">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Hit
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move is not an attack, e.g. is a
             <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
              stance
             </a>
             transition only.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage after the throw.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-ch">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              CH
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Counter_hit" title="Counter hit">
              counter hit
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if this is the same as on normal hit, i.e. there is no special behavior on counter hit.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startupRoot">
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startup">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Startup
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Active_frame" title="Active frame">
              active frames
             </a>
             of the attack. The "i" stands for "impact", i.e. impact
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frame
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             If there is more than one hit, a comma indicates that frame 1 is now the frame after the last active frame of the previous hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , therefore, this usually has a leading comma.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-crush">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              States
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frames
             </a>
             where the attacker is in any special
             <a href="/t/State" title="State">
              states
             </a>
             , e.g.
             <a href="/t/Jump" title="Jump">
              jump
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/t/Parry" title="Parry">
              parry
             </a>
             , or
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Powercrush" title="Powercrush">
              powercrush
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-recv-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-recv">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Recovery
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The total number of
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Recovery" title="Recovery">
               recovery
              </a>
              frames, and what
              <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
               stance
              </a>
              the move recovers in, if any.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              The "t" stands for total and "r" for recovery. If no stance is listed, the move recovers in the default, standing position.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              , the total frame count is from the start of the string with no delays.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-notes">
           <span class="tooltip-label">
            <b>
             Notes
            </b>
           </span>
           <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
            Anything that doesn't fit elsewhere.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            Many common move properties, such as whether a
            <a href="/t/String" title="String">
             string
            </a>
            can be delayed, go here.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            See
            <a href="/t/Movelist#Notes" title="Movelist">
             Movelist#Notes
            </a>
            for standard wording of common properties.
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="b">
           b
          </span>
         </h2>
         <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r23889" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
         <div class="movedata hover-bg-grey-03">
          <div class="movedata-labels">
           <div class="movedata-name has-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Name
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The name of the move in the English localization.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Most often directly from the in-game movelist, but can also be a community name.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Alt
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             Other inputs that also perform this move, written in
             <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
              notation
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-input-ctn">
            <p>
             <span class="movedata-inputLead">
             </span>
             <span class="movedata-input">
              <span class="tooltip-label">
               <b>
                Input
               </b>
              </span>
              <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
               The input to perform the move, written in
               <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
                notation
               </a>
               . This is often used as the move's name.
               <span class="tooltip-hr">
               </span>
               For strings, the input of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
              </span>
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-threat">
           <div class="movedata-target-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-targetLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-target">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Hit level
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a href="/t/Hit_level" title="Hit level">
               hit level
              </a>
              of the move.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Capital letters mean it hits
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Grounded" title="Grounded">
               grounded
              </a>
              .
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the hit level of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-damage-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-damageLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-damage">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Damage
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              How much
              <a href="/t/Damage" title="Damage">
               damage
              </a>
              the move does without any modifiers.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the damage of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-range">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Range
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The maximum
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Range" title="Range">
              range
             </a>
             recorded of the move hitting Lars on-axis. (For
             <i>
              Tekken 7
             </i>
             , it's vs Heihachi.) Assume an error of about Â±0.03.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , this is the range of the whole string.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             This measurement shouldn't on its own be used to compare characters: larger characters get more "range" by this measure, but their
             <i>
              opponents
             </i>
             do too.
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-frames">
           <div class="movedata-tracks left">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Left Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's left.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              right for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-tracks right">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Right Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's right.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              left for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-block">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Block
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on block.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move can't be blocked (e.g., an unblockable or an aerial attack).
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For breakable
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage when the throw is broken.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-hit">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Hit
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move is not an attack, e.g. is a
             <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
              stance
             </a>
             transition only.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage after the throw.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-ch">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              CH
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Counter_hit" title="Counter hit">
              counter hit
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if this is the same as on normal hit, i.e. there is no special behavior on counter hit.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startupRoot">
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startup">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Startup
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Active_frame" title="Active frame">
              active frames
             </a>
             of the attack. The "i" stands for "impact", i.e. impact
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frame
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             If there is more than one hit, a comma indicates that frame 1 is now the frame after the last active frame of the previous hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , therefore, this usually has a leading comma.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-crush">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              States
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frames
             </a>
             where the attacker is in any special
             <a href="/t/State" title="State">
              states
             </a>
             , e.g.
             <a href="/t/Jump" title="Jump">
              jump
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/t/Parry" title="Parry">
              parry
             </a>
             , or
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Powercrush" title="Powercrush">
              powercrush
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-recv-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-recv">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Recovery
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The total number of
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Recovery" title="Recovery">
               recovery
              </a>
              frames, and what
              <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
               stance
              </a>
              the move recovers in, if any.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              The "t" stands for total and "r" for recovery. If no stance is listed, the move recovers in the default, standing position.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              , the total frame count is from the start of the string with no delays.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-notes">
           <span class="tooltip-label">
            <b>
             Notes
            </b>
           </span>
           <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
            Anything that doesn't fit elsewhere.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            Many common move properties, such as whether a
            <a href="/t/String" title="String">
             string
            </a>
            can be delayed, go here.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            See
            <a href="/t/Movelist#Notes" title="Movelist">
             Movelist#Notes
            </a>
            for standard wording of common properties.
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="u">
           u
          </span>
         </h2>
         <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r23889" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
         <div class="movedata hover-bg-grey-03">
          <div class="movedata-labels">
           <div class="movedata-name has-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Name
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The name of the move in the English localization.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Most often directly from the in-game movelist, but can also be a community name.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Alt
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             Other inputs that also perform this move, written in
             <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
              notation
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-input-ctn">
            <p>
             <span class="movedata-inputLead">
             </span>
             <span class="movedata-input">
              <span class="tooltip-label">
               <b>
                Input
               </b>
              </span>
              <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
               The input to perform the move, written in
               <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
                notation
               </a>
               . This is often used as the move's name.
               <span class="tooltip-hr">
               </span>
               For strings, the input of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
              </span>
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-threat">
           <div class="movedata-target-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-targetLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-target">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Hit level
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a href="/t/Hit_level" title="Hit level">
               hit level
              </a>
              of the move.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Capital letters mean it hits
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Grounded" title="Grounded">
               grounded
              </a>
              .
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the hit level of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-damage-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-damageLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-damage">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Damage
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              How much
              <a href="/t/Damage" title="Damage">
               damage
              </a>
              the move does without any modifiers.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the damage of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-range">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Range
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The maximum
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Range" title="Range">
              range
             </a>
             recorded of the move hitting Lars on-axis. (For
             <i>
              Tekken 7
             </i>
             , it's vs Heihachi.) Assume an error of about Â±0.03.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , this is the range of the whole string.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             This measurement shouldn't on its own be used to compare characters: larger characters get more "range" by this measure, but their
             <i>
              opponents
             </i>
             do too.
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-frames">
           <div class="movedata-tracks left">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Left Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's left.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              right for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-tracks right">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Right Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's right.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              left for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-block">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Block
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on block.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move can't be blocked (e.g., an unblockable or an aerial attack).
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For breakable
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage when the throw is broken.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-hit">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Hit
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move is not an attack, e.g. is a
             <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
              stance
             </a>
             transition only.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage after the throw.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-ch">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              CH
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Counter_hit" title="Counter hit">
              counter hit
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if this is the same as on normal hit, i.e. there is no special behavior on counter hit.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startupRoot">
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startup">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Startup
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Active_frame" title="Active frame">
              active frames
             </a>
             of the attack. The "i" stands for "impact", i.e. impact
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frame
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             If there is more than one hit, a comma indicates that frame 1 is now the frame after the last active frame of the previous hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , therefore, this usually has a leading comma.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-crush">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              States
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frames
             </a>
             where the attacker is in any special
             <a href="/t/State" title="State">
              states
             </a>
             , e.g.
             <a href="/t/Jump" title="Jump">
              jump
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/t/Parry" title="Parry">
              parry
             </a>
             , or
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Powercrush" title="Powercrush">
              powercrush
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-recv-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-recv">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Recovery
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The total number of
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Recovery" title="Recovery">
               recovery
              </a>
              frames, and what
              <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
               stance
              </a>
              the move recovers in, if any.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              The "t" stands for total and "r" for recovery. If no stance is listed, the move recovers in the default, standing position.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              , the total frame count is from the start of the string with no delays.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-notes">
           <span class="tooltip-label">
            <b>
             Notes
            </b>
           </span>
           <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
            Anything that doesn't fit elsewhere.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            Many common move properties, such as whether a
            <a href="/t/String" title="String">
             string
            </a>
            can be delayed, go here.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            See
            <a href="/t/Movelist#Notes" title="Movelist">
             Movelist#Notes
            </a>
            for standard wording of common properties.
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>

           <span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File">
            <figure class="embedvideo" data-iframeconfig='{"src":""}' data-service="local-embed" style="width:640px">

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Motion_Input">
           Motion Input
          </span>
         </h2>
         <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r23889" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
         <div class="movedata hover-bg-grey-03">
          <div class="movedata-labels">
           <div class="movedata-name has-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Name
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The name of the move in the English localization.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Most often directly from the in-game movelist, but can also be a community name.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Alt
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             Other inputs that also perform this move, written in
             <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
              notation
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-input-ctn">
            <p>
             <span class="movedata-inputLead">
             </span>
             <span class="movedata-input">
              <span class="tooltip-label">
               <b>
                Input
               </b>
              </span>
              <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
               The input to perform the move, written in
               <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
                notation
               </a>
               . This is often used as the move's name.
               <span class="tooltip-hr">
               </span>
               For strings, the input of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
              </span>
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-threat">
           <div class="movedata-target-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-targetLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-target">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Hit level
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a href="/t/Hit_level" title="Hit level">
               hit level
              </a>
              of the move.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Capital letters mean it hits
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Grounded" title="Grounded">
               grounded
              </a>
              .
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the hit level of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-damage-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-damageLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-damage">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Damage
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              How much
              <a href="/t/Damage" title="Damage">
               damage
              </a>
              the move does without any modifiers.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the damage of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-range">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Range
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The maximum
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Range" title="Range">
              range
             </a>
             recorded of the move hitting Lars on-axis. (For
             <i>
              Tekken 7
             </i>
             , it's vs Heihachi.) Assume an error of about Â±0.03.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , this is the range of the whole string.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             This measurement shouldn't on its own be used to compare characters: larger characters get more "range" by this measure, but their
             <i>
              opponents
             </i>
             do too.
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-frames">
           <div class="movedata-tracks left">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Left Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's left.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              right for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-tracks right">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Right Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's right.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              left for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-block">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Block
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on block.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move can't be blocked (e.g., an unblockable or an aerial attack).
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For breakable
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage when the throw is broken.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-hit">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Hit
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move is not an attack, e.g. is a
             <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
              stance
             </a>
             transition only.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage after the throw.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-ch">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              CH
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Counter_hit" title="Counter hit">
              counter hit
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if this is the same as on normal hit, i.e. there is no special behavior on counter hit.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startupRoot">
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startup">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Startup
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Active_frame" title="Active frame">
              active frames
             </a>
             of the attack. The "i" stands for "impact", i.e. impact
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frame
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             If there is more than one hit, a comma indicates that frame 1 is now the frame after the last active frame of the previous hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , therefore, this usually has a leading comma.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-crush">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              States
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frames
             </a>
             where the attacker is in any special
             <a href="/t/State" title="State">
              states
             </a>
             , e.g.
             <a href="/t/Jump" title="Jump">
              jump
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/t/Parry" title="Parry">
              parry
             </a>
             , or
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Powercrush" title="Powercrush">
              powercrush
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-recv-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-recv">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Recovery
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The total number of
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Recovery" title="Recovery">
               recovery
              </a>
              frames, and what
              <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
               stance
              </a>
              the move recovers in, if any.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              The "t" stands for total and "r" for recovery. If no stance is listed, the move recovers in the default, standing position.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              , the total frame count is from the start of the string with no delays.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-notes">
           <span class="tooltip-label">
            <b>
             Notes
            </b>
           </span>
           <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
            Anything that doesn't fit elsewhere.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            Many common move properties, such as whether a
            <a href="/t/String" title="String">
             string
            </a>
            can be delayed, go here.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            See
            <a href="/t/Movelist#Notes" title="Movelist">
             Movelist#Notes
            </a>
            for standard wording of common properties.
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="WS">
           WS
          </span>
         </h2>
         <link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r23889" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/>
         <div class="movedata hover-bg-grey-03">
          <div class="movedata-labels">
           <div class="movedata-name has-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Name
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The name of the move in the English localization.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Most often directly from the in-game movelist, but can also be a community name.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-alt">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Alt
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             Other inputs that also perform this move, written in
             <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
              notation
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-input-ctn">
            <p>
             <span class="movedata-inputLead">
             </span>
             <span class="movedata-input">
              <span class="tooltip-label">
               <b>
                Input
               </b>
              </span>
              <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
               The input to perform the move, written in
               <a href="/t/Notation" title="Notation">
                notation
               </a>
               . This is often used as the move's name.
               <span class="tooltip-hr">
               </span>
               For strings, the input of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
              </span>
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-threat">
           <div class="movedata-target-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-targetLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-target">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Hit level
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a href="/t/Hit_level" title="Hit level">
               hit level
              </a>
              of the move.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Capital letters mean it hits
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Grounded" title="Grounded">
               grounded
              </a>
              .
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the hit level of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-damage-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-damageLead">
            </span>
            <span class="movedata-damage">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Damage
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              How much
              <a href="/t/Damage" title="Damage">
               damage
              </a>
              the move does without any modifiers.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              ,â€‹ the damage of the previous moves in the string is shown but washed out.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-range">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Range
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The maximum
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Range" title="Range">
              range
             </a>
             recorded of the move hitting Lars on-axis. (For
             <i>
              Tekken 7
             </i>
             , it's vs Heihachi.) Assume an error of about Â±0.03.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , this is the range of the whole string.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             This measurement shouldn't on its own be used to compare characters: larger characters get more "range" by this measure, but their
             <i>
              opponents
             </i>
             do too.
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-frames">
           <div class="movedata-tracks left">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Left Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's left.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              right for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-tracks right">
            <div class="movedata-tracks-label">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Right Tracking
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Tracking_score" title="Tracking score">
               tracking score
              </a>
              to the attacker's right.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              Roughly speaking, when up close, if the defender
              <a href="/t/Sidestep" title="Sidestep">
               sidesteps
              </a>
              or
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Sidewalk" title="Sidewalk">
               sidewalks
              </a>
              left for no more than this many
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the move still connects.
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-block">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Block
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on block.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move can't be blocked (e.g., an unblockable or an aerial attack).
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For breakable
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage when the throw is broken.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-hit">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Hit
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if the move is not an attack, e.g. is a
             <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
              stance
             </a>
             transition only.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/Throw" title="Throw">
              throws
             </a>
             , this is the frame advantage after the throw.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-ch">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              CH
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Frame_advantage" title="Frame advantage">
              frame advantage
             </a>
             on
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Counter_hit" title="Counter hit">
              counter hit
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             Blank if this is the same as on normal hit, i.e. there is no special behavior on counter hit.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startupRoot">
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-startup">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              Startup
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Active_frame" title="Active frame">
              active frames
             </a>
             of the attack. The "i" stands for "impact", i.e. impact
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frame
             </a>
             .
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             If there is more than one hit, a comma indicates that frame 1 is now the frame after the last active frame of the previous hit.
             <span class="tooltip-hr">
             </span>
             For
             <a href="/t/String" title="String">
              strings
             </a>
             , therefore, this usually has a leading comma.
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-crush">
            <span class="tooltip-label">
             <b>
              States
             </b>
            </span>
            <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
             The
             <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
              frames
             </a>
             where the attacker is in any special
             <a href="/t/State" title="State">
              states
             </a>
             , e.g.
             <a href="/t/Jump" title="Jump">
              jump
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="/t/Parry" title="Parry">
              parry
             </a>
             , or
             <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Powercrush" title="Powercrush">
              powercrush
             </a>
             .
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="movedata-recv-ctn">
            <span class="movedata-recv">
             <span class="tooltip-label">
              <b>
               Recovery
              </b>
             </span>
             <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
              The total number of
              <a href="/t/Frame" title="Frame">
               frames
              </a>
              , the
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/t/Recovery" title="Recovery">
               recovery
              </a>
              frames, and what
              <a href="/t/Stance" title="Stance">
               stance
              </a>
              the move recovers in, if any.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              The "t" stands for total and "r" for recovery. If no stance is listed, the move recovers in the default, standing position.
              <span class="tooltip-hr">
              </span>
              For
              <a href="/t/String" title="String">
               strings
              </a>
              , the total frame count is from the start of the string with no delays.
             </span>
            </span>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="movedata-notes">
           <span class="tooltip-label">
            <b>
             Notes
            </b>
           </span>
           <span class="tooltip-body" style="display: none">
            Anything that doesn't fit elsewhere.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            Many common move properties, such as whether a
            <a href="/t/String" title="String">
             string
            </a>
            can be delayed, go here.
            <span class="tooltip-hr">
            </span>
            See
            <a href="/t/Movelist#Notes" title="Movelist">
             Movelist#Notes
            </a>
            for standard wording of common properties.
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
